could occur this winter amid a &#8216;devastating resurgence of virtually eliminated life-threatening diseases&#8217;.\n\n\n\nSenior doctors say a fall in the number of people getting the MMR vaccine has led to a resurgence of the once-rare disease.\n\n\n\nOnly 85% of five-year-olds in England have had the recommended two doses, the lowest in a decade.\n\n\n\nCases have also been reported among teenagers and adults due to historic hesitancy over the vaccine.\n\n\n\nBetween January 1 and June 30 this year there were 128 laboratory confirmed measles cases in England &#8211; compared to 54 cases in the whole of 2022.\n\n\n\nNew guidelines have been drawn up for NHS staff for children with respiratory infections and parents have been urged to &#8216;think measles&#8217;.\n\n\n\nThe Royal College of Paediatrics and Child Health has also asked health professionals to check vaccination records of children entering hospitals.\n\n\n\nThe college also says the vaccine should be promoted to anyone who has not had both doses.\n\n\n\n\n\t\n\t\t\t\n\t\tSymptoms include a rash on the skin (Picture: Getty Images)\n\n\n\n\n\nThere have been measles outbreaks across the UK and Europe, with cases reported in cities including Sheffield, Leicester, Cardiff and London.\n\n\n\nThe UK Health Security Agency (UKHSA) previously warned of an outbreak of between 40,000 and 60,000 in London due to poor uptake.     \n\n\n\nThe World Health Organisation (WHO) also warned of a &#8216;perfect storm&#8217; for a large-scale outbreak.\n\n\n\nRoyal College president Dr Camilla Kingdon warned of winter surges in other infections like flu, Covid and Group A Strep.\n\n\n\n\t\t\n\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\tWhat is Measles? \t\t\t\n\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\tMeasles is an infection that spreads easily and can cause serious problems in some people. Having the MMR vaccine is the best way to prevent it.\nMeasles usually starts with cold-like symptoms, followed by a rash a few days later. Some people may also get small spots in their mouth.\nSymptoms include:\n\na high temperature\na runny or blocked nose\nsneezing\na cough\nred, sore, watery eyes\nspots in the mouth\nmeales rash\n\nAfter seeing a GP, people are advised to:\n\nrest and drink plenty fluids, such as water, to avoid dehydration\ntake paracetamol and ibuprofen to relieve a high temperature but do not give aspirin to children under the age of 16\nuse cotton wool soaked in warm water to gently remove any crusts from your or your child&#8217;s eyes\nStay off nursery, school, or work for at least 4 days from when the rash first appears\nAlso try to avoid close contact with babies, people who are pregnant and people with weakened immune systems\n\n\t\t\t\n\t\t\n\n\n\n\nShe also said: &#8216;Having to consider measles in our national guidance for the first time in decades is a disappointing but necessary move.\n\n\n\n&#8216;Vaccination coverage for children under the age of five is now the lowest it has ever been in the past 10 years.\n\n\n\n&#8216;We are already starting to see the effects of this with measles outbreaks occurring in London, Wales and Leicester.\n\n\n\n&#8216;Many paediatricians I know live in fear of potential measles outbreaks this winter.&#8217;\n\n\n\nGet in touch with our news team by emailing us at webnews@metro.co.uk.\n\n\n\nFor more stories like this, check our news page.","speakable":{"@type":"SpeakableSpecification","xpath":["\/html\/head\/title","\/html\/head\/meta[@name=\"description\"]\/@content"]}}</script>

				<div class="article__content">
					<div class="article__content__inner">
						<figure class="img-container shareable-item wp-caption">
	<div class="img-wrap">
		<img fetchpriority="high" width="646" height="424" src="https://metro.co.uk/wp-content/uploads/2023/11/SEI_152595673-4cd6.jpg?quality=90&amp;strip=all&amp;w=646" class="article-image wp-image-19853477" alt="FILE PHOTO: A vial of the measles, mumps, and rubella (MMR) vaccine is pictured at the International Community Health Services clinic in Seattle, Washington, U.S., March 20, 2019. REUTERS/Lindsey Wasson/File Photo 12516371" decoding="sync">	</div>
		<figcaption>Uptake for the MMR vaccine is at a ten-year low (Picture: Reuters)</figcaption>
</figure><p class="">A major measles outbreak could occur this winter amid a devastating resurgence of virtually eliminated life-threatening diseases.</p>
<p class="">Senior doctors say a fall in the number of people getting the MMR vaccine has led to a resurgence of the once-rare disease.</p>
<p class="">Only 85% of five-year-olds in <a data-ico="hyperlink-article" data-track="inline-tag-auto-link_article" href="https://metro.co.uk/tag/england/?ico=auto_link_news_P3_LNK1">England</a> have had the recommended two doses, the lowest in a decade.</p>
<p class="">Cases have also been reported among teenagers and adults due to historic hesitancy over the vaccine.</p>
<div class="ad-slot ad-slot-container connatix_placeholder_desktop ad-slot-large ad-slot-medium ad-slot-small has-ad-placeholder"><div id="connatix_placeholder_desktop" data-unit="connatix_placeholder_desktop" data-pos="pos"> </div></div><p class="">Between January 1 and June 30 this year there were 128 laboratory confirmed measles cases in England  compared to 54 cases in the whole of 2022.</p>
<p class="">New guidelines have been drawn up for NHS staff for children with respiratory infections and parents have been urged to think measles.</p>
<div class="ad-slot ad-slot-container mpu_mobile_top ad-slot-small has-ad-placeholder"><div id="mpu_mobile_top" data-unit="mpu_mobile_top" data-pos="pos"><script>if(window.adverts) {window.adverts.addToArray({"pos":"mpu_mobile_top"});}</script> </div></div><div class="ad-slot ad-slot-container mpu_tablet ad-slot-medium has-ad-placeholder"><div id="mpu_tablet" data-unit="mpu_tablet" data-pos="pos"><script>if(window.adverts) {window.adverts.addToArray({"pos":"mpu_tablet"});}</script> </div></div><p class="">The Royal College of Paediatrics and Child Health has also asked health professionals to check vaccination records of children entering hospitals.</p>
<p class="">The college also says the vaccine should be promoted to anyone who has not had both doses.</p>
<figure class="img-container shareable-item wp-caption">
	<div class="img-wrap">
		<img width="646" height="431" src="https://metro.co.uk/wp-content/uploads/2023/11/SEI_179150659-209a.jpg?quality=90&amp;strip=all&amp;w=646" class="article-image wp-image-19853634" alt="Sick child with red rash spots from measles." loading="lazy" decoding="async">	</div>
		<figcaption>Symptoms include a rash on the skin (Picture: Getty Images)</figcaption>
</figure><p class="">There have been <a data-ico="hyperlink-article" href="https://metro.co.uk/2023/11/07/measles-outbreak-confirmed-in-england-19786303/">measles outbreaks across the UK and Europe</a>, with cases reported in cities including Sheffield, Leicester, Cardiff and London.</p>
<p class="">The UK Health Security Agency (UKHSA) previously warned of an outbreak of between 40,000 and 60,000 in London due to poor uptake.</p>
<p class="">The World Health Organisation (WHO) also warned of a perfect storm for a large-scale outbreak.</p>
<p class="">Royal College president Dr Camilla Kingdon warned of winter surges in other infections like flu, Covid and Group A Strep.</p>
<div class="factbox" data-ico="factbox_article" data-track-module="factbox_article">
			<h2 class="factbox-title">
				What is Measles? 			</h2>
			<div class="factbox-content">
				<p class="">Measles is an infection that spreads easily and can cause serious problems in some people. Having the MMR vaccine is the best way to prevent it.</p>
<p class="">Measles usually starts with cold-like symptoms, followed by a rash a few days later. Some people may also get small spots in their mouth.</p>
<p class="">Symptoms include:</p>
<ul class="wp-block-list">
<li>a high temperature</li>
<li>a runny or blocked nose</li>
<li>sneezing</li>
<li>a cough</li>
<li>red, sore, watery eyes</li>
<li>spots in the mouth</li>
<li>meales rash</li>
</ul>
<p class="">After seeing a GP, people are advised to:</p>
<ul class="wp-block-list">
<li>rest and drink plenty fluids, such as water, to avoid dehydration</li>
<li>take paracetamol and ibuprofen to relieve a high temperature but do not give aspirin to children under the age of 16</li>
<li>use cotton wool soaked in warm water to gently remove any crusts from your or your childs eyes</li>
<li>Stay off nursery, school, or work for at least 4 days from when the rash first appears</li>
<li>Also try to avoid close contact with babies, people who are pregnant and people with weakened immune systems</li>
</ul>
			</div>
		</div>
<p class="">She also said: Having to consider measles in our national guidance for the first time in decades is a disappointing but necessary move.</p>

<p class="">Vaccination coverage for children under the age of five is now the lowest it has ever been in the past 10 years.</p>
<p class="">We are already starting to see the effects of this with measles outbreaks occurring in London, Wales and Leicester.</p>
<p class="">Many paediatricians I know live in fear of potential measles outbreaks this winter.</p>
